       if(['message','non_field_errors'].includes(key)) \r\n          msg += value + \" \\n \";\r\n        else \r\n          msg += key + \": \" + value + \" \\n \";\r\n      });\r\n      return msg;\r\n    } else {\r\n      return \"Server error, please contact support for more information.\";\r\n    }\r\n  } else if (error.request) {\r\n    // The request was made but no response was received\r\n    // `error.request` is an instance of XMLHttpRequest in the browser and an instance of\r\n    // http.ClientRequest in node.js\r\n     return \"file was successfully uploaded, verify that the information is reflected, if an error has occurred please contact support.\";\r\n  } else {\r\n    // Something happened in setting up the request that triggered an Error\r\n    return
